## Sync to HR Management System

Ways by merchants

The users are grant to access the HR Management Platform such HR Website, iOS and Android Apps after the Sync process have been successful. The login usernames and passwords for HR Platform will be same.

## © Giga Gates. 2026 support@gigagates.com

If you prefer to access the employees who are not included in Delivery Management Platform, you can add into the HR System over the HR website or mobile Apps!

<!-- Britium Express Delivery Service -->

<!-- English -->

![header_image](https://static-us-img.skywork.ai/prod/nexus/1770181357/cropped_image_2_1770181357898883365.jpg)

## Overdue ways count

Overdue ways by

deliveryman

Settings

These settings are effected your system operation. Please reset to default value if you think of abnormal conditions.

Overdue ways by

merchant

- Way ID trailing length *

Total ways by town

The random number of 6 digits will be added to the end of way ID, the minimum length should be 6 digits. (Default is 6)

Merchants order

compare

Promotion code length\(^{*}\)

![image](https://static-us-img.skywork.ai/prod/nexus/1770181357/cropped_image_16_1770181357902949054.jpg)

## ▶ Broadcast message

The promotion code will be generated 6 of random characters and numbers, the minimum length should be 6. (Default is 6)

Create message

— Last pickup hour [24hr format] *

Message list

When the order is received before 15 o'clock, it will be collected on that day, otherwise it will be collected on next day. (Please use 24hr format, default is 12 o'clock)

Facebook pages

Viber bots

— Last deliver hour [24hr format] *

Media files

When the order is received before 12 o'clock, it will be delivered on that day, otherwise it will be delivered on next day. (Please use 24hr format, default is 10 o'clock)

▼ Teams

Return way charges in percentage\(^{*}\)

Branches

Sync users to HRM

When the way is returned, 0% of actual delivery charges will be applied to merchant. (Default is 100)

Zone and auto assign

Customer contact phone number *

9 400 500 542

Station network

If there have any problems or inquiries, 9 400 500 542 phone number will be shown to merchants and customers.

Station coverages

Financial Center

— Maximum station distance [meters] *

7000

HR Management

When the station distance is within 7000 meters, the system will link each other automatically for automatic transit route. (Default is 7000)

— Same day plan hour [24hr format] *

Pricing and package

When the order is received before 12 o'clock, the order will be delivered on Same Day. (Please use 24hr format, default is 10 o'clock)

Regular pricing

![image](https://static-us-img.skywork.ai/prod/nexus/1770181358/cropped_image_48_1770181358482358089.jpg)

Exclusive pricing

Automatically assign the deliveryman for pickup and deliver

Cashback promotion

When the order is created, the deliveryman will be assigned and scheduled based on rotating plan. (Default is enabled)

Code promotion

![image](https://static-us-img.skywork.ai/prod/nexus/1770181358/cropped_image_54_1770181358509848938.jpg)

Automatically create a customer account

When the deliver way is added, the recipient will be created as a user account, so that the recipient can login and track the way. (Default is disable)

## Contacts

Merchant contacts

![image](https://static-us-img.skywork.ai/prod/nexus/1770181358/cropped_image_59_1770181358780660239.jpg)

Automatically add the recipient information into the address book list

Recipient contacts

When the deliver way is added, the recipient information will be added into the address book list, so that this address will be usable on next time. (Default is enable)

Customer support

![image](https://static-us-img.skywork.ai/prod/nexus/1770181358/cropped_image_64_1770181358946961411.jpg)

Allow cash advance for all merchants

When this option is enable, the merchant will see the Cash Advance option while creating the order. (Default is enable)

Settings

Bank list

![image](https://static-us-img.skywork.ai/prod/nexus/1770181359/cropped_image_69_1770181359024751101.jpg)

## Allow merchant direct order

System settings

When this option is enable, all merchants can submit the order themselves. (Default is enable)

Highway gate list

Allow merchant direct order auto assign

When the merchant submits the order for pickup, the deliveryman will be assigned and scheduled automatically. (Default is disable)

Places of interest

Town list

## Allow merchant direct delivery way fill

Edit Terms &

When you enable this option, your all merchants can fill the delivery way information themselves. (Default is enable)

Conditions

![image](https://static-us-img.skywork.ai/prod/nexus/1770181359/cropped_image_83_1770181359148106539.jpg)

Allow merchant direct way fill auto assign

Audit logs

When the merchant fills the delivery way information, the deliveryman will be assigned and scheduled automatically. (Default is disable)

(1) Logout

Remind refund money on next pickup

When you create a pickup for specific merchant and you may require to refund to that merchant, the reminder message will be shown. (Default is enable)
